                                <option value="@cat">@cat</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="categoryChips">
                            @foreach (var cat in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Categories)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="create-chip @(Model.Category == cat ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cat" data-target="categorySelect">
                                    @cat
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="categoryErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Condition *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label class="create-field__label">Condition</label>
                        <select asp-for="Condition" class="create-hidden-select" id="conditionSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <option value="@cond">@cond</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-condition" id="conditionPills">
                            @{
                                var icons = new[] { "✦", "★", "◆", "▲", "●" };
                                var idx = 0;
                            }
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-condition__pill @(Model.Condition == cond ? "create-condition__pill--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cond" data-target="conditionSelect">
                                    <span>@icons[idx]</span> <span>@cond</span>
                                </button>
                                idx++;
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="conditionErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Size — optional *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label class="create-field__label">Size</label>
                            <span class="create-field__optional">optional</span>
                        </div>
                        <select asp-for="Size" class="create-hidden-select" id="sizeSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <option value="@size">@size</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="sizeChips">
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-chip @(Model.Size == size ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@size" data-target="sizeSelect">
                                    @size
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Stealable Listing Section ─────────────────────────── *@
                    <div class="create-field create-field--stealable">
                        <div class="create-stealable-header">
                            <div>
                                <p class="create-field__label">Listing Type</p>
                                <p class="create-stealable-header__sub">
                                    Stealable listings let buyers compete — one claims it, another can steal it.
                                </p>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        <label class="stealable-toggle" for="IsStealable">
                            <span class="stealable-toggle__track">
                                <input asp-for="IsStealable" id="IsStealable" type="checkbox"
                                       class="stealable-toggle__input" />
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__thumb" aria-hidden="true"></span>
                            </span>
                            <span class="stealable-toggle__label-group">
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__name">Make this a Stealable listing</span>
                                <span class="stealable-toggle__badge" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="11" height="11">
                                        <path d="M8.75 3.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v3.5h-3.5a.75.75 0 000 1.5h3.5v3.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-3.5h3.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.5v-3.5z" />
                                    </svg>
                                    NEW
                                </span>
                            </span>
                        </label>

                        <div class="stealable-duration-panel" id="stealDurationPanel"
                             @(Model.IsStealable ? "" : "hidden") aria-live="polite">
                            <div class="stealable-duration-inner">
                                <svg class="stealable-duration-icon" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm.75-13a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v5c0 .414.336.75.75.75h4a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.25V5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                <div class="stealable-duration-body">
                                    <label asp-for="StealDurationHours" class="create-field__label">Steal Window Duration</label>
                                    <p class="stealable-duration-body__hint">
                                        How long a buyer has before another can steal the item.
                                        After the window closes, the original buyer gets a 2-hour grace period.
                                    </p>
                                    <select asp-for="StealDurationHours" class="create-hidden-select" id="stealDurationSelect">
                                        <option value=""></option>
                                        @foreach (var hours in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.StealDurations)
                                        {
                                            <option value="@hours">@hours hours</option>
                                        }
                                    </select>
                                    <div class="create-chips" id="durationChips">
                                        @foreach (var hours in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemCreateViewModel.StealDurations)
                                        {
                                            <button type="button"
                                                    class="create-chip @(Model.StealDurationHours == hours ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                                    data-value="@hours" data-target="stealDurationSelect">
                                                @hours hr
                                            </button>
                                        }
                                    </div>
                                    <span class="field__error" id="durationErr"></span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* Actions *@
                    <div class="create-actions">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary" id="submitBtn">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                                <path d="M10 1a9 9 0 100 18A9 9 0 0010 1zm4.53 6.03l-5 5a.75.75 0 01-1.06 0l-2-2a.75.75 0 111.06-1.06l1.47 1.47 4.47-4.47a.75.75 0 111.06 1.06z" />
                            </svg>
                            Post Listing
                        </button>
                        <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                    </div>

                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{
        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");
    }

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var MAX_PHOTOS = 5;
            var fileList   = new DataTransfer(); // virtual file list maintained by JS

            // ── DOM refs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var addZone    = document.getElementById('photoAddZone');
            var photosInput = document.getElementById('photosInput');
            var thumbsEl   = document.getElementById('photoThumbs');
            var photoErr   = document.getElementById('photoErr');
            var form       = document.getElementById('createForm');
            var submitBtn  = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            var banner     = document.getElementById('validationBanner');
            var bannerText = document.getElementById('validationBannerText');

            // ── Photo: add zone click / drag ──────────────────────────────────────
            addZone.addEventListener('click', function () { photosInput.click(); });

            addZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
                addFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
            });

            photosInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var selectedFiles = Array.from(photosInput.files); // capture BEFORE clearing
                photosInput.value = '';                            // reset native picker
                addFiles(selectedFiles);                           // syncInput runs last → files stay
            });

            function addFiles(files) {
                var errors = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                    if (fileList.files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) break;
                    var f = files[i];
                    if (!['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp'].includes(f.type)) {
                        errors.push('Only JPEG, PNG, or WebP images are accepted.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (f.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        errors.push(f.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    fileList.items.add(f);
                }
                if (errors.length) photoErr.textContent = errors[0];
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function removeFile(idx) {
                var newDt = new DataTransfer();
                Array.from(fileList.files).forEach(function (f, i) {
                    if (i !== idx) newDt.items.add(f);
                });
                fileList = newDt;
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function syncInput() {
                photosInput.files = fileList.files;
            }

            function renderThumbs() {
                thumbsEl.innerHTML = '';
                var files = Array.from(fileList.files);
                files.forEach(function (file, i) {
                    var div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'photo-thumb';

                    var img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.alt = 'Photo ' + (i + 1);
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function (e) { img.src = e.target.result; };
                    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                    div.appendChild(img);

                    if (i === 0) {
                        var badge = document.createElement('span');
                        badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge';
                        badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                        div.appendChild(badge);
                    }

                    var rm = document.createElement('button');
                    rm.type = 'button';
                    rm.className = 'photo-thumb__remove';
                    rm.innerHTML = '×';
                    rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove photo');
                    (function (idx) {
                        rm.addEventListener('click', function () { removeFile(idx); });
                    }(i));
                    div.appendChild(rm);

                    thumbsEl.appendChild(div);
                });

                // Show/hide add zone
                if (files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) {
                    addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                } else {
                    addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                }

                // Clear photo error when thumbs are present
                if (files.length > 0) photoErr.textContent = '';
            }

            // ── Character counters ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                var input   = document.getElementById(inputId);
                var counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                if (!input || !counter) return;
                var update = function () {
                    var len = input.value.length;
                    counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                    counter.classList.toggle('create-field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                };
                input.addEventListener('input', update);
                update();
            }
            initCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
            initCounter('descInput',  'descCounter',  1000);

            // ── Required chips (category, condition) ──────────────────────────────
            function initChips(containerId) {
                var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (!container) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var select = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
                    if (!select) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active','create-condition__pill--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add(containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'create-chip--active' : 'create-condition__pill--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    // Clear the error for this field
                    var errId = containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'categoryErr' : 'conditionErr';
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }
            initChips('categoryChips');
            initChips('conditionPills');

            // ── Optional chips (size) — second click deselects ────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('sizeChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('sizeSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var already = btn.classList.contains('create-chip--active');
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    if (already) { select.value = ''; }
                    else { btn.classList.add('create-chip--active'); select.value = btn.dataset.value; }
                });
            }());

            // ── Duration chips ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('durationChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add('create-chip--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    var errEl = document.getElementById('durationErr');
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }());

            // ── Stealable toggle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var checkbox = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                var panel    = document.getElementById('stealDurationPanel');
                var durSel   = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!checkbox || !panel) return;
                function sync() {
                    if (checkbox.checked) {
                        panel.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    } else {
                        panel.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                        if (durSel) { durSel.value = ''; }
                        document.querySelectorAll('#durationChips [data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                            b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                        });
                    }
                }
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', sync);
                sync();
            }());

            // ── Auto-clear input errors on change ────────────────────────────────
            function bindClearError(inputId, errId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (!el) return;
                el.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    el.classList.remove('input-error');
                    if (wrapId) document.getElementById(wrapId) && document.getElementById(wrapId).classList.remove('input-error');
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    if (banner.style.display !== 'none') {
                        // Re-check if any errors remain
                        var anyErr = document.querySelectorAll('.input-error, .chips-error, .field__error:not(:empty)').length;
                        if (!anyErr) banner.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            }
            bindClearError('titleInput', 'titleErr');
            bindClearError('descInput',  'descErr');
            bindClearError('priceInput', 'priceErr', 'priceWrap');

            // ── Client-side form validation ───────────────────────────────────────
            function showErr(errId, msg) {
                var el = document.getElementById(errId);
                if (el) el.textContent = msg;
            }
            function markInputErr(inputId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('input-error');
                if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.add('input-error'); }
                return el;
            }
            function markChipsErr(containerId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('chips-error');
                return el;
            }

            function validate() {
                var firstErrEl = null;
                var ok = true;

                // Clear previous
                ['titleErr','descErr','priceErr','categoryErr','conditionErr','durationErr','photoErr'].forEach(function (id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '';
                });
                document.querySelectorAll('.input-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('input-error'); });
                document.querySelectorAll('.chips-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('chips-error'); });

                // Title
                var titleEl = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                var titleLen = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (titleLen < 3 || titleLen > 100) {
                    showErr('titleErr', 'Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('titleInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Description
                var descEl = document.getElementById('descInput');
                var descLen = descEl ? descEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (descLen < 10 || descLen > 1000) {
                    showErr('descErr', 'Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('descInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Price
                var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                var priceVal = priceEl ? parseFloat(priceEl.value) : NaN;
                if (!priceEl || !priceEl.value || isNaN(priceVal) || priceVal < 0.01 || priceVal > 99999.99) {
                    showErr('priceErr', 'Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('priceInput', 'priceWrap');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Category
                var catSel = document.getElementById('categorySelect');
                if (!catSel || !catSel.value) {
                    showErr('categoryErr', 'Please select a category.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('categoryChips');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Condition
                var condSel = document.getElementById('conditionSelect');
                if (!condSel || !condSel.value) {
                    showErr('conditionErr', 'Please select a condition.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('conditionPills');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Steal duration
                var stealChk = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                if (stealChk && stealChk.checked) {
                    var durSel = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                    if (!durSel || !durSel.value) {
                        showErr('durationErr', 'Please select a Steal window duration.');
                        firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('durationChips');
                        ok = false;
                    }
                }

                if (!ok) {
                    banner.style.display = 'flex';
                    if (firstErrEl) firstErrEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                } else {
                    banner.style.display = 'none';
                }

                return ok;
            }

            // ── Submit handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault(); // Always prevent — let our validate() decide
                if (!validate()) return;
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<svg class="spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".25"/></svg> Posting…';
                form.submit(); // Programmatic submit bypasses event listeners
            });

            // ── Auto-dismiss toast ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var toast = document.querySelector('.create-toast');
            if (toast) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    toast.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                }, 4000);
            }

        }());
    </script>
}

--- Views/Items/Details.cshtml ---

@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = Model.Title;
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";

    bool isOwner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOwner ?? false);
    bool isAnonymous = (bool)(ViewBag.IsAnonymous ?? true);
    bool isCurrentWinner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsCurrentWinner ?? false);
    bool isOriginalGetter = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOriginalGetter ?? false);

    bool isStealable = Model.ListingType == ListingType.Stealable;
    bool stealWindowOpen = isStealable
                           && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved
                           && Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue
                           && DateTime.UtcNow <= Model.StealEndsAt.Value;

    string sellerDisplay = Model.User is not null
        ? Model.User.Email.Split('@')[0]
        : "Unknown seller";

    string condClass = Model.Condition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };

    string priceLabel = isStealable ? "Starting price" : "Fixed price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved)
        priceLabel = "Current price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
        priceLabel = "Stolen price";

    bool hasImages = Model.ImageUrls.Count > 0;
}

<div class="detail-shell">

    @* ── Back navigation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
    <nav class="detail-breadcrumb" aria-label="Breadcrumb">
        <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="detail-breadcrumb__link">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" aria-hidden="true">

            @if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)

            @if (isOwner)

                <div class="detail-actions">

                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M.458 10C1.732 5.943 5.522 3 10 3s8.268 2.943 9.542 7c-1.274 4.057-5.064 7-9.542 7S1.732 14.057.458 10zM14 10a4 4 0 11-8 0 4 4 0 018 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>

                @* ══ 3d. Stealable — StolenPendingCheckout ══
                         The stealer has bumped the price and is mid-checkout.
                         They can complete or cancel. Others see a waiting notice. *@
                else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
                {
                    @if (isCurrentWinner)
                    {
                        <div class="detail-actions">
                            <a asp-action="Checkout" asp-controller="Orders" asp-route-itemId="@Model.Id"

                                </svg>
                                Complete Purchase
                            </a>

                            You stole this item at ₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2"). Complete your

                    }
                    else if (isOriginalGetter)
                    {
                        @* Original getter: reassure them their reservation is intact *@
                        <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">
                            <div class="detail-winner-notice">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">

                                </svg>

                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <div class="detail-actions detail-actions--waiting">

                                </svg>
                                <span>A buyer is completing a steal purchase. If they cancel, the item returns to its previous holder.</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    }
                }

                @if (TempData["InfoMessage"] is string infoMsg)
                {
                    <div class="create-toast create-toast--info">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                        </svg>
                        @infoMsg
                    </div>
                }

                @* ══ 3e. Stealable — Sold (order confirmed) ══ *@
                else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Sold)
                {
                    @* Sold notice is rendered above; no button needed unless still pending *@
                }


            }

        </section>

    </div>

</div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            // ── Gallery (runs only when multi-image elements exist) ───────────────
            (function () {
                var mainImg   = document.getElementById('mainGalleryImg');
                var thumbsEl  = document.getElementById('galleryThumbs');
                var prevBtn   = document.getElementById('galleryPrev');
                var nextBtn   = document.getElementById('galleryNext');
                var counterEl = document.getElementById('galleryCounter');

                // Early-exit is now safely scoped inside a nested IIFE
                // so it does NOT kill the countdown timers below.
                if (!mainImg || !thumbsEl) return;

                var thumbBtns = Array.prototype.slice.call(thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('.gallery-thumb'));
                var total     = thumbBtns.length;
                var current   = 0;

                function goTo(idx) {
                    if (idx === current) return;
                    mainImg.classList.add('gallery-fading');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        mainImg.src = thumbBtns[idx].dataset.src;
                        mainImg.classList.remove('gallery-fading');
                    }, 200);
                    thumbBtns[current].classList.remove('gallery-thumb--active');
                    thumbBtns[idx].classList.add('gallery-thumb--active');
                    if (counterEl) counterEl.textContent = (idx + 1) + ' / ' + total;
                    current = idx;
                }

                thumbBtns.forEach(function (btn, i) {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo(i); });
                });
                if (prevBtn) prevBtn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo((current - 1 + total) % total); });
                if (nextBtn) nextBtn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo((current + 1) % total); });

                document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  goTo((current - 1 + total) % total);
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') goTo((current + 1) % total);
                });

                var touchStartX = null;
                mainImg.addEventListener('touchstart', function (e) {
                    touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                }, { passive: true });
                mainImg.addEventListener('touchend', function (e) {
                    if (touchStartX === null) return;
                    var dx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - touchStartX;
                    touchStartX = null;
                    if (Math.abs(dx) < 40) return;
                    if (dx < 0) goTo((current + 1) % total);
                    else        goTo((current - 1 + total) % total);
                }, { passive: true });
            }());

            // ── Countdown timers — always run regardless of gallery state ─────────
            function startCountdown(el) {
                if (!el) return;
                var endsAt = new Date(el.dataset.endsAt);
                if (endsAt <= new Date()) { el.textContent = '00:00:00'; return; }
                var intervalId = null;
                function tick() {
                    var diffMs = endsAt - new Date();
                    if (diffMs <= 0) {
                        el.textContent = '00:00:00';
                        clearInterval(intervalId);
                        window.location.reload();
                        return;
                    }
                    var s = Math.floor(diffMs / 1000);
                    var h = Math.floor(s / 3600);
                    var m = Math.floor((s % 3600) / 60);
                    el.textContent =
                        String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' +
                        String(m).padStart(2, '0') + ':' +
                        String(s % 60).padStart(2, '0');
                }
                tick();
                intervalId = setInterval(tick, 1000);
            }

            // These run unconditionally — the bug was they were inside the gallery IIFE.
            startCountdown(document.getElementById('stealTimer'));
            startCountdown(document.getElementById('finalizeTimer'));

            // ── How-it-works modals ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            var TODAY = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

            function wasDismissedToday(key) {
                try { return localStorage.getItem(key) === TODAY; } catch(e) { return false; }
            }
            function dismissForToday(key) {
                try { localStorage.setItem(key, TODAY); } catch(e) {}
            }

            function initModal(opts) {
                var overlay    = document.getElementById(opts.overlayId);
                var proceedBtn = document.getElementById(opts.proceedId);
                var dismissChk = document.getElementById(opts.dismissCheckId);
                var triggers   = document.querySelectorAll(opts.triggerSelector);

                if (!overlay || !triggers.length) return;

                function showModal() {
                    overlay.classList.add('hiw-overlay--visible');
                    if (proceedBtn) proceedBtn.focus();
                }
                function hideModal() {
                    overlay.classList.remove('hiw-overlay--visible');
                }
                function proceed() {
                    if (dismissChk && dismissChk.checked) dismissForToday(opts.storageKey);
                    hideModal();
                    opts.onProceed();
                }

                triggers.forEach(function (trigger) {
                    var form = trigger.closest('form');
                    if (form) {
                        form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                            if (wasDismissedToday(opts.storageKey)) return;
                            e.preventDefault();
                            showModal();
                            opts.onProceed = function () { form.submit(); };
                        });
                    }
                });

                if (proceedBtn) proceedBtn.addEventListener('click', proceed);
                overlay.addEventListener('click', function (e) { if (e.target === overlay) hideModal(); });
                document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                    if (e.key === 'Escape' && overlay.classList.contains('hiw-overlay--visible')) hideModal();
                });
            }

            initModal({
                storageKey:      'thriftloop_hiw_get',
                overlayId:       'hiwGetOverlay',
                proceedId:       'hiwGetProceed',
                dismissCheckId:  'hiwGetDismiss',
                triggerSelector: 'form[action*="GetItem"] button[type="submit"]',
                onProceed:       function () {}
            });

            initModal({
                storageKey:      'thriftloop_hiw_steal',
                overlayId:       'hiwStealOverlay',
                proceedId:       'hiwStealProceed',
                dismissCheckId:  'hiwStealDismiss',
                triggerSelector: 'form[action*="StealItem"] button[type="submit"]',
                onProceed:       function () {}
            });

        }());
    </script>
}

                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label asp-for="Description" class="create-field__label">Description</label>
                            <span class="create-field__counter" id="descCounter">0/1000</span>
                        </div>
                        <textarea asp-for="Description" class="create-field__input create-field__input--textarea"
                                  id="descInput" rows="3" maxlength="1000"
                                  placeholder="Describe the item — colour, fit, any flaws…"></textarea>
                        <span class="field__error" id="descErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Price *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label asp-for="Price" class="create-field__label">Price (₱)</label>
                        <div class="create-price-wrap" id="priceWrap">
                            <span class="create-price-wrap__symbol">₱</span>
                            <input asp-for="Price" id="priceInput"
                                   class="create-field__input create-price-wrap__input"
                                   type="number" step="0.01" min="0.01" max="99999.99" placeholder="0.00" />
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="priceErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Category *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label class="create-field__label">Category</label>
                        <select asp-for="Category" class="create-hidden-select" id="categorySelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var cat in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Categories)
                            {
                                <option value="@cat">@cat</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="categoryChips">
                            @foreach (var cat in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Categories)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-chip @(Model.Category == cat ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cat" data-target="categorySelect">
                                    @cat
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="categoryErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Condition *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <label class="create-field__label">Condition</label>
                        <select asp-for="Condition" class="create-hidden-select" id="conditionSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <option value="@cond">@cond</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-condition" id="conditionPills">
                            @foreach (var cond in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Conditions)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-condition__pill @(Model.Condition == cond ? "create-condition__pill--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@cond" data-target="conditionSelect">
                                    @cond
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                        <span class="field__error" id="conditionErr"></span>
                    </div>

                    @* Size — optional *@
                    <div class="create-field">
                        <div class="create-field__top">
                            <label class="create-field__label">Size</label>
                            <span class="create-field__optional">optional</span>
                        </div>
                        <select asp-for="Size" class="create-hidden-select" id="sizeSelect">
                            <option value=""></option>
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <option value="@size">@size</option>
                            }
                        </select>
                        <div class="create-chips" id="sizeChips">
                            @foreach (var size in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.ItemEditViewModel.Sizes)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="create-chip @(Model.Size == size ? "create-chip--active" : "")"
                                        data-value="@size" data-target="sizeSelect">
                                    @size
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* Actions *@
                    <div class="create-actions">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn--primary" id="submitBtn">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                            </svg>
                            Save Changes
                        </button>
                        <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                    </div>

                </div>
            </div>
        </form>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{
        await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");
    }

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var MAX_PHOTOS = 5;
            var newFileList = new DataTransfer(); // new uploads only

            // ── DOM refs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var form         = document.getElementById('editForm');
            var thumbsEl     = document.getElementById('photoThumbs');
            var addZone      = document.getElementById('photoAddZone');
            var newInput     = document.getElementById('newPhotosInput');
            var photoErr     = document.getElementById('photoErr');
            var submitBtn    = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            var banner       = document.getElementById('validationBanner');
            var bannerText   = document.getElementById('validationBannerText');

            // ── Helpers: count totals ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            function existingCount() {
                return thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('[data-existing]').length;
            }
            function totalCount() {
                return existingCount() + newFileList.files.length;
            }

            // ── Existing image removal ────────────────────────────────────────────
            // Delegate on thumbsEl so it catches server-rendered buttons.
            thumbsEl.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                var btn = e.target.closest('[data-existing-url]');
                if (!btn) return;

                var url = btn.getAttribute('data-existing-url');

                // 1. Remove the thumbnail div
                var thumb = btn.closest('[data-existing]');
                if (thumb) thumb.remove();

                // 2. Remove the matching ExistingImageUrls hidden input
                var inputs = form.querySelectorAll('.existing-url-input');
                inputs.forEach(function (inp) {
                    if (inp.value === url) inp.remove();
                });

                // 3. Inject a RemovedImageUrls hidden input so the controller knows to delete the file
                var rmInp = document.createElement('input');
                rmInp.type  = 'hidden';
                rmInp.name  = 'RemovedImageUrls';
                rmInp.value = url;
                form.appendChild(rmInp);

                updateCoverBadge();
                updateAddZone();
            });

            // Reapply "Cover" badge to the new first thumb after any removal
            function updateCoverBadge() {
                thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('.photo-thumb__badge').forEach(function (b) { b.remove(); });
                var firstThumb = thumbsEl.querySelector('.photo-thumb');
                if (firstThumb) {
                    var badge = document.createElement('span');
                    badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge';
                    badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                    firstThumb.appendChild(badge);
                }
            }

            function updateAddZone() {
                if (totalCount() >= MAX_PHOTOS) {
                    addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                } else {
                    addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                }
            }

            // ── New image upload ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            addZone.addEventListener('click', function () { newInput.click(); });

            addZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
                addNewFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
            });

            newInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var selectedFiles = Array.from(newInput.files);
                newInput.value = '';
                addNewFiles(selectedFiles);
            });

            function addNewFiles(files) {
                var errors = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                    if (totalCount() >= MAX_PHOTOS) break;
                    var f = files[i];
                    if (!['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp'].includes(f.type)) {
                        errors.push('Only JPEG, PNG, or WebP images are accepted.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (f.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        errors.push(f.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    newFileList.items.add(f);
                    appendNewThumb(f, newFileList.files.length - 1);
                }
                if (errors.length) photoErr.textContent = errors[0];
                newInput.files = newFileList.files;
                updateAddZone();
                updateCoverBadge();
            }

            function appendNewThumb(file, idx) {
                var div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'photo-thumb photo-thumb--new';

                var img = document.createElement('img');
                img.alt = 'New photo';
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function (e) { img.src = e.target.result; };
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                div.appendChild(img);

                var badge = document.createElement('span');
                badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge photo-thumb__badge--new';
                badge.textContent = 'New';
                div.appendChild(badge);

                var rm = document.createElement('button');
                rm.type = 'button';
                rm.className = 'photo-thumb__remove';
                rm.innerHTML = '×';
                rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove new photo');
                rm.addEventListener('click', function () { removeNewThumb(div, idx); });
                div.appendChild(rm);

                thumbsEl.appendChild(div);
            }

            function removeNewThumb(div, removeIdx) {
                var newDt = new DataTransfer();
                Array.from(newFileList.files).forEach(function (f, i) {
                    if (i !== removeIdx) newDt.items.add(f);
                });
                newFileList = newDt;
                newInput.files = newFileList.files;
                div.remove();
                updateAddZone();
                updateCoverBadge();
            }

            // ── Character counters ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                var input   = document.getElementById(inputId);
                var counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                if (!input || !counter) return;
                var update = function () {
                    var len = input.value.length;
                    counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                    counter.classList.toggle('create-field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                };
                input.addEventListener('input', update);
                update();
            }
            initCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
            initCounter('descInput',  'descCounter',  1000);

            // ── Required chips ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initChips(containerId) {
                var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (!container) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var select = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
                    if (!select) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active','create-condition__pill--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add(containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'create-chip--active' : 'create-condition__pill--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    var errId = containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'categoryErr' : 'conditionErr';
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }
            initChips('categoryChips');
            initChips('conditionPills');

            // ── Size chips (optional) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('sizeChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('sizeSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var already = btn.classList.contains('create-chip--active');
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('create-chip--active'); });
                    if (already) { select.value = ''; }
                    else { btn.classList.add('create-chip--active'); select.value = btn.dataset.value; }
                });
            }());

            // ── Auto-clear input errors ───────────────────────────────────────────
            function bindClearError(inputId, errId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (!el) return;
                el.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    el.classList.remove('input-error');
                    if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.remove('input-error'); }
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                });
            }
            bindClearError('titleInput', 'titleErr');
            bindClearError('descInput',  'descErr');
            bindClearError('priceInput', 'priceErr', 'priceWrap');

            // ── Client-side form validation ───────────────────────────────────────
            function showErr(errId, msg) { var el = document.getElementById(errId); if (el) el.textContent = msg; }
            function markInputErr(inputId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('input-error');
                if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.add('input-error'); }
                return el;
            }
            function markChipsErr(containerId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('chips-error');
                return el;
            }

            function validate() {
                var firstErrEl = null;
                var ok = true;

                ['titleErr','descErr','priceErr','categoryErr','conditionErr'].forEach(function (id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '';
                });
                document.querySelectorAll('.input-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('input-error'); });
                document.querySelectorAll('.chips-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('chips-error'); });

                var titleEl = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                var titleLen = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (titleLen < 3 || titleLen > 100) {
                    showErr('titleErr', 'Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('titleInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var descEl = document.getElementById('descInput');
                var descLen = descEl ? descEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (descLen < 10 || descLen > 1000) {
                    showErr('descErr', 'Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('descInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                var priceVal = priceEl ? parseFloat(priceEl.value) : NaN;
                if (!priceEl || !priceEl.value || isNaN(priceVal) || priceVal < 0.01 || priceVal > 99999.99) {
                    showErr('priceErr', 'Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('priceInput', 'priceWrap');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var catSel = document.getElementById('categorySelect');
                if (!catSel || !catSel.value) {
                    showErr('categoryErr', 'Please select a category.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('categoryChips');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var condSel = document.getElementById('conditionSelect');
                if (!condSel || !condSel.value) {
                    showErr('conditionErr', 'Please select a condition.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('conditionPills');
                    ok = false;
                }

                if (!ok) {
                    banner.style.display = 'flex';
                    if (firstErrEl) firstErrEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                } else {
                    banner.style.display = 'none';
                }

                return ok;
            }

            // ── Submit handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (!validate()) return;
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<svg class="spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".25"/></svg> Saving…';
                form.submit();
            });

        }());
    </script>
}

        public void OnGet()
        {
        }
    }
}

}

<div class="container">

        @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string successMsg)
        {

                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />

                <span>@successMsg</span>
            </div>
        }

        @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
        {
            <div class="create-error-banner" style="margin-bottom:1rem">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">

            </div>
        }

        <div class="listings-header">
            <div>
                <h1 class="listings-header__title">My Listings</h1>
                <p class="listings-header__subtitle">
                    @if (Model.Count == 1)
                    {
                        <span>You have <strong>1</strong> active listing</span>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <span>You have <strong>@Model.Count</strong> active listings</span>
                    }
                </p>
            </div>
            <a asp-action="Create" class="btn btn--primary">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">
                    <path d="M10.75 4.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5h-4.5a.75.75 0 000 1.5h4.5v4.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5h4.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-4.5v-4.5z" />
                </svg>
                New Listing
            </a>
        </div>

        @if (!Model.Any())
        {
            <div class="listings-empty">
                <div class="listings-empty__icon">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5">
                        <rect x="8" y="10" width="32" height="32" rx="4" />
                        <path d="M16 10V8a4 4 0 018 0v2M24 22v8M20 26h8" />
                    </svg>
                </div>
                <h2 class="listings-empty__title">No listings yet</h2>
                <p class="listings-empty__body">
                    Post your first item and start earning from things you no longer need.
                </p>
                <a asp-action="Create" class="btn btn--primary">Post your first item</a>
            </div>
        }
        else
        {
            <div class="listings-table-wrap">
                @*
                    Each <tr> carries data-href pointing to the Details page.
                    A JS delegated-click handler (at the bottom of this file) navigates
                    there when the click target is NOT a link, button, or form element,
                    so Edit / Delete still work independently.
                    cursor:pointer is applied via the listings-row--clickable CSS class.

                                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()

                                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">

                            </tr>

                    </tbody>
                </table>
            </div>
        }
    </div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            // ── Toast auto-dismiss ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            var toast = document.querySelector('.listings-toast');
            if (toast) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    toast.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                }, 4000);
            }

            // ── Clickable rows ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
            // Navigate to the Details page when the user clicks anywhere on a row
            // that is NOT an interactive element (link, button, or form).
            var rows = document.querySelectorAll('.listings-row--clickable');

            rows.forEach(function (row) {
                row.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    // Walk up from the click target — if we hit an interactive element
                    // before reaching the row itself, let the browser handle it normally.
                    if (e.target.closest('a, button, input, form')) return;

                    var href = row.dataset.href;
                    if (href) window.location.href = href;
                });
            });

        }());
    </script>
}

        .co-pay-options {
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            gap: 0.625rem;
        }

        .co-pay-option {
            display: flex;
            align-items: flex-start;

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var radios      = document.querySelectorAll('.co-pay-radio');
            var hiddenInput = document.getElementById('paymentMethodInput');
            var form        = document.getElementById('confirmForm');
            var btn         = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');

            radios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (hiddenInput) hiddenInput.value = radio.value;
                });
            });

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.innerHTML =
                        '<svg class="co-spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" ' +
                        'width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">' +
                        '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".3"/>' +
                        '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 017 7h-1.5A5.5 5.5 0 0010 4.5V3z"/>' +
                        '</svg> Confirming\u2026';
                });

--- Views/Orders/MyPurchases.cshtml ---

@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Order>
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "My Purchases";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
}

<div class="mp-shell">

    <header class="mp-header">
        <div>
            <h1 class="mp-header__title">My Purchases</h1>
            <p class="mp-header__subtitle">
                @Model.Count order@(Model.Count == 1 ? "" : "s") placed
            </p>
        </div>
        <div class="mp-header__actions">
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Wallet" class="btn btn--ghost mp-wallet-link">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="15" height="15" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M1 4.25a3.733 3.733 0 012-.575h13.5c.43 0 .845.069 1.232.198A2.25 2.25 0 0015.5 3h-11a3 3 0 00-3 3v1.25H1V4.25z" />
                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 8.5v6A2.5 2.5 0 003.5 17h13a2.5 2.5 0 002.5-2.5v-6A2.5 2.5 0 0016.5 6h-13A2.5 2.5 0 001 8.5zm14.5 3a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                </svg>
                My Wallet
            </a>
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--ghost mp-header__cta">
                Browse listings
            </a>
        </div>
    </header>

    @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string successMsg)
    {
        <div class="mp-toast mp-toast--success" id="mpToast" role="status">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            @successMsg
        </div>
    }
    @if (TempData["InfoMessage"] is string infoMsg)
    {
        <div class="mp-toast mp-toast--info" id="mpToast" role="status">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a.75.75 0 000 1.5h.253a.25.25 0 01.244.304l-.459 2.066A1.75 1.75 0 0010.747 15H11a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-.253a.25.25 0 01-.244-.304l.459-2.066A1.75 1.75 0 009.253 9H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
            </svg>
            @infoMsg
        </div>
    }
    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
    {
        <div class="mp-toast mp-toast--error" id="mpToast" role="alert">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">

            </svg>
            @errMsg
        </div>
    }

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="mp-empty">
            <div class="mp-empty__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                    <rect x="8" y="16" width="48" height="36" rx="6" />
                    <path d="M22 16v-4a10 10 0 0120 0v4" stroke-linecap="round" />
                    <path d="M24 36h16" stroke-linecap="round" />
                </svg>
            </div>
            <h2 class="mp-empty__title">No purchases yet</h2>
            <p class="mp-empty__body">Items you confirm will appear here.</p>
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--primary mp-empty__cta">
                Browse listings
            </a>
        </div>
    }
    else
    {
        <div class="mp-list">
            @foreach (var order in Model)
            {
                var sellerEmail = order.Seller?.Email ?? string.Empty;
                var sellerDisplay = sellerEmail.Contains('@') ? sellerEmail.Split('@')[0] : sellerEmail;

                string statusClass = order.Status switch
                {
                    OrderStatus.Pending => "mp-status--pending",
                    OrderStatus.Completed => "mp-status--completed",
                    OrderStatus.Cancelled => "mp-status--cancelled",
                    _ => ""
                };

                string statusLabel = order.Status switch
                {
                    OrderStatus.Pending => "Pending",
                    OrderStatus.Completed => "Completed",
                    OrderStatus.Cancelled => "Cancelled",
                    _ => order.Status.ToString()
                };

                string payLabel = order.PaymentMethod switch
                {
                    PaymentMethod.Wallet => "Wallet (escrow)",
                    PaymentMethod.Cash => "Cash on Delivery",
                    _ => order.PaymentMethod.ToString()
                };

                bool canMarkDelivered = order.Status == OrderStatus.Pending;

                <article class="mp-row">

                    <div class="mp-row__img-wrap">
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(order.Item?.ImageUrl))
                        {
                            <img src="@order.Item.ImageUrl" alt="@order.Item?.Title"
                                 class="mp-row__img" loading="lazy" />
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="mp-row__img mp-row__img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                    <rect x="3" y="5" width="26" height="22" rx="3" />
                                    <circle cx="11" cy="13" r="3" />
                                    <path d="M3 23l8-7 5 5 4-3 9 7" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                            </div>
                        }
                    </div>

                    <div class="mp-row__body">
                        <div class="mp-row__top">
                            <h3 class="mp-row__title">
                                @(order.Item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order.ItemId)
                            </h3>
                            <span class="mp-status @statusClass">@statusLabel</span>
                        </div>

                        <p class="mp-row__seller">Seller: @sellerDisplay</p>

                        @* Payment method pill *@
                        <p class="mp-row__pay">
                            <span class="mp-pay-pill mp-pay-pill--@(order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet ? "wallet" : "cod")">
                                @if (order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet)
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3.5A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 2h9A1.5 1.5 0 0113 3.5v7A1.5 1.5 0 0111.5 12h-9A1.5 1.5 0 011 10.5v-7zm10.5 2.5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                                    </svg>
                                }
                                @payLabel
                            </span>
                        </p>

                        <p class="mp-row__date">
                            Ordered
                            <time datetime="@order.OrderDate.ToString("yyyy-MM-ddTHH:mm:ssZ")">
                                @order.OrderDate.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                            </time>
                        </p>

                        @* Mark Delivered — only visible on Pending orders *@
                        @if (canMarkDelivered)
                        {
                            <form asp-action="MarkDelivered"
                                  asp-controller="Orders"
                                  asp-route-orderId="@order.Id"
                                  method="post"
                                  class="mp-deliver-form"
                                  onsubmit="return confirm('Confirm delivery of this order? This will release payment to the seller.');">
                                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                <button type="submit" class="mp-deliver-btn">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                    I received this item
                                </button>
                            </form>
                        }
                    </div>

                    <div class="mp-row__price-col">
                        <span class="mp-row__price">₱@order.FinalPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                        <span class="mp-row__price-label">Final price</span>
                    </div>

                </article>
            }
        </div>
    }

</div>

@section Scripts {

    Swapping to <strong>Development</strong> environment will display more detailed information about the error that occurred.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>The Development environment shouldn't be enabled for deployed applications.</strong>
    It can result in displaying sensitive information from exceptions to end users.
    For local debugging, enable the <strong>Development</strong> environment by setting the <strong>ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT</strong> environment variable to <strong>Development</strong>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();

                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            // Close dropdown when clicking outside
            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var input   = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var form    = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn     = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var presets = document.querySelectorAll('.addfunds-quick__btn');

            presets.forEach(function (p) {
                p.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!input) return;
                    input.value = p.dataset.amount;
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    p.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                });
            });

            if (input) {
                input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    presets.forEach(function (b) {
                        if (b.dataset.amount === input.value) b.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                    });
                });
            }

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

            height: 36px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 10%, transparent);
            color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            flex-shrink: 0;
        }

        .wd-method-option__name {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.9rem;
            font-weight: 600;
            color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
            margin: 0 0 1px;
        }

        .wd-method-option__hint {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.78rem;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            margin: 0;
        }

        .wd-submit {
            width: 100%;
            justify-content: center;
        }
    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

/* --------------------------------------------- */
/* ThriftLoop - Master Stylesheet                */
/* Design System: compact, accessible, consistent */

:root {
    /* Colors - high contrast for accessibility */
    --c-primary: #2d1b69; /* deep purple - WCAG AA compliant on white */
    --c-primary-light: #3d2880; /* hover state */
    --c-primary-soft: #e9e5f5; /* background tint */
    --c-bg: #f2f2f5; /* page background */
    --c-surface: #ffffff; /* cards, panels */
    --c-border: #e4e4ea; /* borders and dividers */
    --c-text: #111118; /* main body - high contrast */
    --c-muted: #4b4b63; /* secondary text - improved contrast */
    --c-muted-light: #8f8fa3; /* placeholder text */
    --c-badge-bg: #ece8f8; /* badge background */
    --c-badge-txt: #2d1b69; /* badge text */
